	OutputLine(NULL, "　魅音は司法なんかに身を委ねずに、…自らの手で幕を下ろすかもしれない。",
		   NULL, "Mion podia não entregar-se à justiça... então eu mesmo podia ter de colocar um fim a isso.", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }


//　......レナは、すでにそこまで読んでいた￥
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　……レナは、すでにそこまで読んでいた。",
		   NULL, "......Rena já tinha pensado bem longe.", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

//「あぁ＠......そんなこと、絶対にさせないから。＠
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#956f6e>圭一</color>", NULL, "<color=#956f6e>Keiichi</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 1, "ps3/s02/01/130101063", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「あぁ。",
		   NULL, "\"Certo.", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 1, "ps3/s02/01/130101064", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "……そんなこと、絶対にさせないから。」",
		   NULL, " ...Eu não vou deixar isso acontecer.\"", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }


//　レナがいつの間にか溜めていた涙を、擦る￥
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　レナがいつの間にか溜めていた涙を、擦る。",
		   NULL, "Rena esfregou suas lágrimas, que tinham caído sem ela perceber", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();
	DisableWindow();
	ModDrawCharacter(3, 2, "sprite/re1a_warai_a1_", "2", 160, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 20, 200, TRUE );

//「じゃあ...行ってあげて。＠
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#f0953d>レナ</color>", NULL, "<color=#f0953d>Rena</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 2, "ps3/s02/02/130200582", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「じゃあ…行ってあげて。」",
		   NULL, "\"Ok... então, vá junto com ela.\"", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }


//　頷き、玄関へ消えた魅音を追う￥
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　頷き、玄関へ消えた魅音を追う。",
		   NULL, "Eu assenti e segui Mion, que tinha desaparecido pela porta da frente.", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();
	DisableWindow();
	DrawSceneWithMask("background/rouka1", "left", 0, 0, 300 );


//　......ふすまの向こうから聞こえるレナの嗚咽が、はっきりと聞こえた￥
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　……ふすまの向こうから聞こえるレナの嗚咽が、はっきりと聞こえた。",
		   NULL, "...Eu podia ouvir claramente Rena soluçando do outro lado da porta de papel.", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

//　.........どうして魅ぃちゃんは、......鬼なんか継がされちゃったんだろうね＠
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#f0953d>レナ</color>", NULL, "<color=#f0953d>Rena</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 2, "ps3/s02/02/130200583", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「………どうして魅ぃちゃんは、……鬼なんか継がされちゃったんだろうね。",
		   NULL, "\"......Por que Mii-chan era... a sucessora dos demônios?", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }


//　...それは仕方のないことだったんだろうね...＠
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#f0953d>レナ</color>", NULL, "<color=#f0953d>Rena</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 2, "ps3/s02/02/130200584", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　…それは仕方のないことだったんだろうね…。",
		   NULL, "...Talvez simplesmente tivesse de ser assim...", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }


//　.........でも、!w1000......あんまりにも!w1000.........可哀想だよね.....................＠
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#f0953d>レナ</color>", NULL, "<color=#f0953d>Rena</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 2, "ps3/s02/02/130200585", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　………でも、",
		   NULL, "......Mas...", Line_ContinueAfterTyping);

	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
	Wait( 1000 );
	SetValidityOfInput( TRUE );

	OutputLine(NULL, "……あんまりにも",
		   NULL, " Isso era simplesmente......", Line_ContinueAfterTyping);

	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
	Wait( 1000 );
	SetValidityOfInput( TRUE );

	OutputLine(NULL, "………可哀想だよね…………………。」",
		   NULL, " digno de pena............\"", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

//　頬を熱いものがぼろりと流れ落ちる＠.........俺の涙だった￥
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　頬を熱いものがぼろりと流れ落ちる。",
		   NULL, "Alguma coisa quente queimava meu rosto.", Line_WaitForInput);
	OutputLine(NULL, "………俺の涙だった。",
		   NULL, " ......Eram minhas lágrimas.", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

//　俺はそれを乱暴に拭う＠
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　俺はそれを乱暴に拭う。",
		   NULL, "Eu as enxuguei com força.", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }


//　......魅音に捧げられる最後の時間に、涙なんか絶対に見せたくなかったから＠
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　……魅音に捧げられる最後の時間に、涙なんか絶対に見せたくなかったから。",
		   NULL, "...Este seriam os últimos minutos eu poderia oferecer à Mion, então eu absolutamente não queria deixá-la ver minhas lágrimas nesse tempo.", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

//　もう魅音は玄関の外で待っていた............￥
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　もう魅音は玄関の外で待っていた…………。",
		   NULL, "Mion já estava esperando do lado de fora da porta da frente.........", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

//if %kaisou_mode = 1 goto *kaisou_mode
	DisableWindow();
	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
	Wait( 1000 );
	DrawBustshotWithFiltering(6, "cinema", "x", 1, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 25, 1300, TRUE );
	DrawBustshot(7, "title02", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 26, 3000, TRUE );
	Wait( 2000 );
	DrawBustshot(5, "black", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 25, 3000, TRUE );
	Wait( 2000 );
	FadeBustshotWithFiltering( 7, "x", 1, FALSE, 0, 0, 1000, TRUE );
	DrawScene("black", 1000 );
	SetValidityOfInput( TRUE );

}
